1A  - G   27933— 32  (06/2018)
   THE  SRI  LANKA   ARMED   SERVICES   LONG   SERVICE   MEDAL
IT is hereby notified that His Excellency the President of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and the Commander
in Chief of the Armed Forces has been pleased to award the Sri Lanka Armed Services Long Service Medal to the persons
specified in the schedule hereto.
                                    By His Excellency’s Command,
Kapila Waidyarathne,P.C.
Secretary,
 Ministry of Defence.
Ministry of Defence,
Colombo,
24th May, 2018.
SCHEDULE
Sri Lanka Armed Services Long Service Medal Officers - Regular Force
Ser. Reg. No. Rank Name Regiment
1 O/60640 BRIG L WIJESUNDARA SLAGSC
